{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="app-intention.js">\n// Quantum Intention Manifestation System - Core JavaScript\n\n// ============================================\n// PARTICLE SYSTEM\n// ============================================\n\nclass ParticleSystem {\n    constructor() {\n        this.canvas = document.getElementById(\'particleCanvas\');\n        this.ctx = this.canvas.getContext(\'2d\');\n        this.particles = [];\n        this.particleCount = 50;\n        this.isTyping = false;\n        \n        this.resize();\n        this.init();\n        this.animate();\n        \n        window.addEventListener(\'resize\', () => this.resize());\n    }\n    \n    resize() {\n        this.canvas.width = window.innerWidth;\n        this.canvas.height = window.innerHeight;\n    }\n    \n    init() {\n        this.particles = [];\n        for (let i = 0; i < this.particleCount; i++) {\n            this.particles.push({\n                x: Math.random() * this.canvas.width,\n                y: Math.random() * this.canvas.height,\n                vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,\n                vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,\n                size: Math.random() * 2 + 1,\n                color: Math.random() > 0.5 ? \'#00FFFF\' : \'#FF00FF\',\n                alpha: Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.2\n            });\n        }\n    }\n    \n    animate() {\n        this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);\n        \n        // Update and draw particles\n        this.particles.forEach(particle => {\n            // Update position\n            particle.x += particle.vx;\n            particle.y += particle.vy;\n            \n            // Wrap around edges\n            if (particle.x < 0) particle.x = this.canvas.width;\n            if (particle.x > this.canvas.width) particle.x = 0;\n            if (particle.y < 0) particle.y = this.canvas.height;\n            if (particle.y > this.canvas.height) particle.y = 0;\n            \n            // Draw particle\n            this.ctx.beginPath();\n            this.ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            this.ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;\n            this.ctx.globalAlpha = particle.alpha;\n            this.ctx.fill();\n            \n            // Add glow effect when typing\n            if (this.isTyping) {\n                this.ctx.shadowBlur = 20;\n                this.ctx.shadowColor = particle.color;\n            } else {\n                this.ctx.shadowBlur = 10;\n            }\n        });\n        \n        // Draw connections\n        this.particles.forEach((p1, i) => {\n            this.particles.slice(i + 1).forEach(p2 => {\n                const dx = p1.x - p2.x;\n                const dy = p1.y - p2.y;\n                const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n                \n                if (distance < 150) {\n                    this.ctx.beginPath();\n                    this.ctx.moveTo(p1.x, p1.y);\n                    this.ctx.lineTo(p2.x, p2.y);\n                    this.ctx.strokeStyle = \'#00FFFF\';\n                    this.ctx.globalAlpha = (1 - distance / 150) * 0.2;\n                    this.ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n                    this.ctx.stroke();\n                }\n            });\n        });\n        \n        this.ctx.globalAlpha = 1;\n        this.ctx.shadowBlur = 0;\n        \n        requestAnimationFrame(() => this.animate());\n    }\n    \n    burst(x, y) {\n        // Create burst effect at specific location\n        for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {\n            const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / 20;\n            const speed = Math.random() * 3 + 2;\n            this.particles.push({\n                x: x,\n                y: y,\n                vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed,\n                vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed,\n                size: Math.random() * 3 + 2,\n                color: Math.random() > 0.5 ? \'#00FFFF\' : \'#FF00FF\',\n                alpha: 1,\n                life: 60\n            });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// INTENTION MANAGER\n// ============================================\n\nclass IntentionManager {\n ============================================\n\nclass ParticleSystem {\n    constructor() {\n        this.canvas = document.getElementById(\'particleCanvas\');\n        this.ctx = => this.resize());\n    }\n    \n    resize() {\n        this.canvas.width = window.innerWidth;\n        this.canvas.height = window.innerHeight;\n    }\n    \n    init() {\n        for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {\n            this.particles.push({\n                x: Math.random() * this.canvas.width,\n                y: Math.random() * this.canvas.height,\n                vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 1,\n                vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 1,\n                size: Math.random() * 3 + 1,\n                color: Math.random() > 0.5 ? \'#00FFFF\' : \'#FF00FF\',\n                alpha: Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.3\n            });\n        }\n    }\n    \n    animate() {\n        this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);\n        \n        this.particles.forEach(particle => {\n            particle.x += particle.vx;\n            particle.y += particle.vy;\n            \n            if (particle.x < 0) particle.x = this.canvas.width;\n            if (particle.x > this.canvas.width) particle.x = 0;\n            if (particle.y < 0) particle.y = this.canvas.height;\n            if (particle.y > this.canvas.height) particle.y = 0;\n            \n            this.ctx.beginPath();\n            this.ctx.arc(particle.x, particle.y, particle.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            this.ctx.fillStyle = particle.color;\n            this.ctx.globalAlpha = particle.alpha;\n            this.ctx.shadowBlur = 15;\n            this.ctx.shadowColor = particle.color;\n            this.ctx.fill();\n        });\n        \n        this.ctx.globalAlpha = 1;\n        this.ctx.shadowBlur = 0;\n        \n        requestAnimationFrame(() => this.animate());\n    }\n    \n    burst(x, y, color) {\n        for (let i = 0; i < 30; i++) {\n            const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / 30;\n            const speed = Math.random() * 5 + 3;\n            this.particles.push({\n                x: x,\n                y: y,\n                vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed,\n                vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed,\n                size: Math.random() * 4 + 2,\n                color: color || \'#00FFFF\',\n                alpha: 1,\n
